  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c22412e4-8fc9-41a0-81f5-b5a7fbd44f88'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText2580678312775957883" style="display:none"><b>From the New York Times bestselling author who brought you the Lords of the Underworld comes a dark, seductive new series featuring angels poised on the brink of destruction.... </b><br /><br />Leader of the most powerful army in the heavens, Zacharel has been deemed nearly too dangerous, too ruthless-and if he isn't careful, he'll lose his wings. But this warrior with a heart of ice will not be deterred from his missions, at any cost...until a vulnerable human tempts him with a carnal pleasure he's never known before. <br /><br />Accused of a crime she did not commit, Annabelle Miller has spent four years in an institution for the criminally insane. Demons track her every move, and their king will stop at nothing to have her. Zacharel is her only hope for survival, but is the brutal angel with a touch as hot as hell her salvation-or her ultimate damnation?</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer228077028" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18321886260388315720"><b>4 stars</b><br/><br/>Wicked Nights, is the first book of Angels of The Dark, spin-off series from Lords of The Underworld.<br/><br/>Annabelle Miller accused as murderer, and insane. 4 years after the the death of her parents, now she become patient of asylum and endure humiliating things done to her while she actually innocent. Worse, demon track her everywhere, and she never know why. Since Annabelle just a mere human. All change after she met this cold-than-ice angel, Zacharel.<br/><br/>Zacharel is one of the warrior angels an</span>
  <span id="freeText18321886260388315720" style="display:none"><b>4 stars</b><br><br>Wicked Nights, is the first book of Angels of The Dark, spin-off series from Lords of The Underworld.<br><br>Annabelle Miller accused as murderer, and insane. 4 years after the the death of her parents, now she become patient of asylum and endure humiliating things done to her while she actually innocent. Worse, demon track her everywhere, and she never know why. Since Annabelle just a mere human. All change after she met this cold-than-ice angel, Zacharel.<br><br>Zacharel is one of the warrior angels and we know about him from Amun's book, The Darkest Secret. His Deity is disappointed with Zacharel's act to murder demon possesed people,even they proven innocent. Zacharel must lead bad behaving angel army or they all will fallen and succumb to the darkness. First meet with Annabelle rose his long dead emotion and passion. Even then he realize Annabele had been marked by High Lord Demon and become its consort, no demons or angels can't stop him to claim Annabelle as his. Now,with demon hot in their tails, Zacharel and Annabelle must find whose demon that target her and ready to face the big war at Heaven and Hell.<br><br>Yes, Gena never disappoint me. But I hope she not use the same theme (human-immortal), since the ending is easily predictable.Its make me a little bored since I will know what happen in the end, even Gena give readers some twist that lead us to the next book, Beauty Awakened.<br><br>What I love from this book is the characterization. Both Annabelle and Zacharel are easily to loved and adore. Annabelle with her strong personality but deep inside she still fragile after all people she love left her. Zacharel who is... oh, did I forget to mention, he's VIRGIN?? Well, dayum! Virgin hero is one of my favorite, since I always love see their woman lover is their first and last. But not just the fact he's still virgin. Zacharel is alpha, infuriated alpha but he don't hesitate to said sorry. His scene when he cry and ask forgiveness to Annabelle is one of my favorite.<br><br>Others characters is likeable too. The angel army feat Thane, Koldo, Xerxes, Bjorn, Axel and Jamila is more likely will be told in the next books. And LOTU fans will happy and rejoice, since the Lords become cameo here, and not just cameo, they have important role too. My disappointment is just I have to see the Harpies again. Sorry, they are my less favorite creatures in LOTU world.<br><br>LOTU and Gena fans will ravish this book and love each page of it. Strong characters, full action, fast pace. Even the ending kinda overused, I assure you still can enjoy this. But I suggest to read the Lords of The Underworld first to know the background and some already known characters. Are the angels hotter than the Lords? Well, you must read this book to prove it by yourself ;)<br><br>BTW, look for my fantasy cast, both for Zacharel and Annabelle :<br><br><b>Zacharel</b> :<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380361991i/713080.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ummm, hotness overload? ;)<br><br><b>Annabelle Miller</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380361991i/713081.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Annabelle is half Japanese half Americans. I want to use Devon Aoki pics, but decide she's too much older for Annabelle that 22 years old.<br><br><br><b>Review for the cover </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379765538i/237994._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="800" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy Moley Naked Batman!!!<br>When I think The Darkest Seduction is the hottest LOTU cover, Zacharel's book steal the attention!!The background look too simple, just plain black, but the model pose are outstanding! Look at those abs! Yummilicious! Think if this angel finally find his wicked side?<br>Pairing of human and angel, I guess in the end the heroine will be immortal, or vice versa. Just sayin ;P<br><br>Note : I'm glad Gena make a new heroine for Zacharel.No more harpies, please!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="18321886260388315720" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11994008351656315486">*checks cover*<br/>*checks blurb*<br/><br/>I thought this was a romance. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473991108ra/20540349.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>261 pages and NO sexy times?!?!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473991053ra/20540345.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm done. Around chapter seventeen, the demons came in more and I think it started to get better, but I just <i>didn't car</i></span>
  <span id="freeText11994008351656315486" style="display:none">*checks cover*<br>*checks blurb*<br><br>I thought this was a romance. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473991108ra/20540349.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>261 pages and NO sexy times?!?!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473991053ra/20540345.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm done. DNF.<br><br>Seriously, NO ROMANCE needs to be over <b>400 pages long.</b> The story CAN'T be that good, and it isn't here. Seriously. Most of this is filler.<br><br>I can't even be bothered to find the scene where they FINALLY consummate their twu wuv. So boring.<br><br>It started good, but then... filler. Major padding. Around chapter seventeen, the demons came in more and I think it started to get better, but I just <i>didn't care anymore.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473991053ra/20540346.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The other angels kind of intrigued me, but I have no interest in continuing the series. I know Gena Showalter has another series (LOTU). This was my first book by her and probably my last. It ended up being just another boring, formulaic PNR. I'm about to write off the whole genre. <br><br>There is nothing wrong with the writing, but there is nothing special about it, and I just don't care.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473991053ra/20540347.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you are into PNR and like "bad boy" angels, you'll probably like this. But this is NOT smutty. So don't be expecting steamy scenes. <br><br><b>20% romance + 30% world-building + 50% filler = BORING BORING BORING.</b><br><br>:P</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=they-are-so-awesome-hot-and-stuff">they-are-so-awesome-hot-and-stuff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer546928437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3198742583738308341"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “It shall be my pleasure to remedy it. First, it is not your strength or your speed that draws me. It's your... everything. Your laugh, your wit, your emotions and the way they change. Your courage, your sweetness, your near obsessive delight in cookies. Second, you are indeed a prize. You've made me want what no one else ever had. A communion of bodies." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>※ update: I did some editing of the review on 17/10/14.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>One word: AMAZING!</i>
</b> I felt skeptical about readi</span>
  <span id="freeText3198742583738308341" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “It shall be my pleasure to remedy it. First, it is not your strength or your speed that draws me. It's your... everything. Your laugh, your wit, your emotions and the way they change. Your courage, your sweetness, your near obsessive delight in cookies. Second, you are indeed a prize. You've made me want what no one else ever had. A communion of bodies." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>※ update: I did some editing of the review on 17/10/14.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>One word: AMAZING!</i>
</b> I felt skeptical about reading it, mostly because it's connected to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/476543.The_Darkest_Night__Lords_of_the_Underworld___1_" title="The Darkest Night (Lords of the Underworld, #1) by Gena Showalter" rel="nofollow noopener">Lords of the Underworld</a>. Actually, only the characters are connected with LoU - so it really isn't necessary to read LOU first. (But because of this book i will definitely read LOU now). And it's my first Gena Showalter experience!<br><br>Anyway, this story was sweet, funny and sometimes tragic, but still amazing book! The characters were just so intriguing and i can't wait to read more about them. <br><br>The world building is quite interesting, and i liked Hierarchy and i really loved Army of Disgrace. This is a story of Angels and Demons, or actually Sent Ones and Demons. There is a certain hierarchy. The Most High ruled the heavens (Merciful One, the Anointed One and the Mighty One are the tree ruling members, going by the name of The Most High). They had appointed several underlings and one of them is Deity Germanus. Germanus is a lesser king, who leads the Elite Seven—Zacharel, Lysander, Andrian, Gabek, Shalilah, Luanne, Svana and they all lead their own armies. Zacharel leads the Army of Disgrace, and he is the main character of this story. <br><br>Since this is a story of Sent One and Demons, then here is a bit more about them: Sent Ones are like angels, but not really. They are adopted children of the Most High, and their lives are tethered to Them. They are the source of their power and essential for their own existence. Angels are lesser in the hierarchy and they are servants and messengers. <br><br>There are many types of the demons and all of them did different things. They also had ranks and they liked to attach themselves to humans or posses them. Demons fed off the panic and upset, thus weakening humans and making them easy target. <br><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>CHARACTERS</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>Zacharel</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://shinhbang.deviantart.com/art/Sinful-Angel-Josh-Kloss-244791010" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411277i/807389._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><a href="http://shinhbang.deviantart.com/art/Sinful-Angel-Josh-Kloss-244791010" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinful Angel - Josh Kloss</a> by ~<a href="http://shinhbang.deviantart.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">shinhbang</a><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “You know, you’re pretty when you smile,” she said, patting the side of his cheek.<br>“Fierce, woman. I am fierce.”<br>“If you say so.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Sexy Angel in charge of a complete mess of an army! He didn't care for the lives of the humans, especially when they were possessed by demons. He killed them, and for that he was punished to lead the worst army of Angels ever. They are all close to falling, and it's up to him to stop that happening. Most of his army doesn't care about anything, and some of them kill human or two, and for those deaths he gets punished. That fact changed his mind about killing humans or letting his army kill them. And then....he meets Annabelle, and saves her. And then some sparkles happen... and a lot of things.<br><br>He also tries to be emotionless - when someone he loved died, he closed off so he could not suffer all of that grief again. Basically, he is very cold character at first. Did i mention that he is extremely arrogant, kick ass, and quite interesting. Also has a gentle side, is a fierce warrior. He is also a virgin! A VIRGIN! VIRGIN! How rare it is for this genre. But i really loved him, and he felt guilt, remorse and regret for some things that he had done, especially to what he had done to Anna accidentally. <br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>Annabelle</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411277i/807390._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Look, Winged Wonder. Get me out of here, then we'll hammer out the details about where I'm staying. Okay?"<br>"Winged Wonder," he said, nodding. "I find that I do not mind that one. It fits."<br>"Captain Modesty fits better," she muttered.<br>"I disagree. Winged Wonder is clearly the better choice for a man such as me." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Annabelle was attacked on her 18th birthday by a Demon. He killed her parents, violated her and hurt her. In shock and despair, she said to everyone that the monster killed her parents, and they judged her to be criminally insane and unstable. Not even her brother believed her. No one did. In just one night she lost everything and was thrown into institution for the criminally insane, and four years have passed from then. While she could see - because her eyes turned colorless and pale - and could feel the demons, the demons sensed her to and hurt her many many times. And because of that, doctors still thought she was insane and that she was trying to hurt herself, despite her efforts to convince them otherwise. Enter Fitzpervert who used her situation to his own benefit. And then, one night, Zachariel finds her, and after lot of convincing, and a lot of calling him names such as Winged Wonder and so on, he finally rescues her and takes her to his home.<br><br>She is a fighter, she will never go without a fight, extremely brave as well, she tries to turn situations in her advantage, she is traumatized, but she doesn't show it easily. She doesn't trust easily either! She is also half Japanese. She was a strong and brave heroine, and overall, great.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>Others</i>
</b>:<br><br>There were many great characters as well. I liked <b>Thane, Xerxes and Bjorn,</b> they are very interesting characters and I want to know more about them. They met and bonded while they were in the captivity of the demons. They are all damaged, and still have side effects from it, because of which they were put in Zachariel's army. They love each other, and they would do anything for each other forever and ever.<br><br><b> Koldo </b> on the other hand i found quite amazing. His wings were torn when he was young, and he never could regenerate them since. But it doesn't make him any less deadly. I couldn't believe what he had gone through for a person he knows for only 3 months - he gave up on something he cherished so much so he could help. He is just...amazing... I am glad the next book is with him!<br><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>OVERALL</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br><i>
  <b>I loved it! It was just... great and i loved everything about it. Can't wait to see what sequels have in store!</b>
</i><br>____________________________________________<br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br>____________________________________________ <br><br><br><b> MY ANGELS OF THE DARK REVIEWS: </b><br><br> ◉ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/546928437" rel="nofollow noopener"> Wicked Nights (Angels of the Dark, #1)</a><br> ◉ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/546928444" rel="nofollow noopener"> Beauty Awakened (Angels of the Dark, #2) </a><br> ◉ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/598120586" rel="nofollow noopener"> Burning Dawn (Angels of the Dark, #3) </a><br><br><b>

<div id="review_271500472" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/271500472" />
    <a title="Neyra ♦" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6872601-neyra"><img alt="Neyra ♦" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442631049p2/6872601.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/271500472?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Neyra ♦" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Neyra ♦" href="/user/show/6872601-neyra">Neyra ♦</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">ALL LOTU &amp; ANGEL PNR FANS :D</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6872601-neyra?shelf=best-of-2012">best-of-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6872601-neyra?shelf=adult-pnr">adult-pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer271500472" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13538322705155478971"><i>
  <b>Actual Rating: 4.5</b>
</i><br/><br/>What I really loved about Wicked Nights was the slow building of the romance. The change in Zacharel, his curiosity, Anabelle's determination, her tenacity. To be honest it's a slow read, more an introduction to the world of the Angels of the Dark, but I found I did not mind. I didn't want to jump into a story where I had no idea what was going on and everything needed to be explained at once so I could play catch up, making it even more confusing. Heartbreaking as it is he</span>
  <span id="freeText13538322705155478971" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Actual Rating: 4.5</b>
</i><br><br>What I really loved about Wicked Nights was the slow building of the romance. The change in Zacharel, his curiosity, Anabelle's determination, her tenacity. To be honest it's a slow read, more an introduction to the world of the Angels of the Dark, but I found I did not mind. I didn't want to jump into a story where I had no idea what was going on and everything needed to be explained at once so I could play catch up, making it even more confusing. Heartbreaking as it is heartwarming, Gena Showalter brings us another amazing series, and beautiful angels on the brink of destruction with no hope for redemption. <br><br>Zacharel, leader of the Army of Disgrace, as his fellow brethren have deemed them, is a cold, heartless, and emotionless angel. When we first met Zacharel in The Darkest Secret, I was immediately intrigued. He is as beautiful and magnetic as he is cold and callous. But how can an angel who is suppose to be kind, compassionate, and caring be so heartless? What has made this angel so icy? When I discovered his reason, I was both shocked and heartbroken, it wasn't something I'd expect to read, but there it was. But all that changes when he meets Anabelle Miller, a human who intrigues the angel like nothing or no one ever has before. To watch him fall apart and contradict himself with her was so beautiful and not to mention hilarious, I couldn't help but fall in love even more with him.<br><br>Anabelle Miller is a human locked up in a criminally insane institution. She's been accused of murdering her parents claiming a demon did it. But what the police doesn't understand, is she is telling the truth. But why is she the only human who can see demons? This was a startling revelation, I had no idea a demon could have a consort, let alone that they could do it whilst the person was dreaming. What I liked about Anabelle? Despite the fact that she was wrongfully accused and living out a life sentence in an insane asylum, she was strong and determined not to go down without a fight, both with the demons and humans alike. I really liked that about her. Then her wry sense of humor with Zacharel, their banter was hilarious. And I like that she doesn't fall head over heels in love with him and let's him treat her like she's beneath him, despite that she's human. <br><br>I liked the slow building of their relationship, it seemed much more realistic that they took things slow, as it was Zacharel's first time, EVER with a woman. I wouldn't go as far as saying the sex scenes were awesome and they were so steamy, no, rather they were endearing and sweet. Not what I was use to from Gena Showalter, but definitely not disappointing either.<br><br>All love aside, though, Zacharel struggles to earn the respect of his men. They're all angels who've seen far more than any other has. And they've been stripped of their humanity, their compassion, their ability to feel anything but the need for destruction and vengeance. I really loved Thane, Bjorn, Xerxes, Koldo, and Axel, though we only see very little of him. I would have liked to see more of the army, and more of their reluctance to heed orders, I mean they're suppose to be the baddest of the bad, right? <br><br>On top of leading an army, Zacharel must deal with demons who are bent on capturing Anabelle for the Demon High Lord, Unforgiveness. But I couldn't help feel disappointed that the reason <i>why</i> he wanted her was so obvious. Still, I liked the end result. And the more I read, the more I wanted to know more. Despite the Angel's new mission to keep from falling, and the battles with demons they must face, there is still the impending war we saw brewing in the Lords of the Underworld series. And I really liked that we got to see the Lords interact with Zacharel again, brief as it was. <br><br>I can't wait to read Koldo's book, which is <i>Beauty Awakened</i>, and read more about the angels. This series is looking very promising and I'd recommend to any LOTU fan and lover of angel paranormal romances :D<br><br><br><br><i>And now for my Fangirl review</i> Well, more like a play by play of my reaction to some of the things that happened :P<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>I'd give this book 5 stars because it was so amazing and I love Zacharel to death! I don't care how cold and heartless he's been in the LOTU books, he's so beautiful, how the hell can you resist!! x] <br><br>Reactions throughout the book:<br><br>Chapter Two- Zacharel and Thane's interaction -<br><br>"Sir, your Great and Mighty Highness? Are You Listening to Me?<br>The masculine voice drew Zacharel from the past and the only bright light in an otherwise dark life, jerking him straight into the present. He glance at Thane, the self-appointed second in command of his angelic army. <br><br>He cleared his throat.<br>"I'm listening, yes." Now.<br>"My humblest apologies if I bored you before" was Thane's flippant reply.<br><br>"I'm eager to fight Majesty. We all are."<br>"I've told you before not to call me by that title. As for your request, you will wait as ordered. All of you" <br><br><b>My Reaction: </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368885ra/721452.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love you already Thane, you're hilarious!<br><br><br>Chapter Seven -Zacharel's interaction with Hadrenial-<br><br>"I love you, Zacharel."<br>"I love you too, Hadrenial. So much."<br>"Do you?"<br>"You know I do."<br>"And you would do anything for me?"<br>"Anything"<br>"Kill me then. A true death. Please. You can't leave me like this."<br>"Like This" had been broken, bloody and violated in unspeakable ways. "Anything but that. You'll recover. One day you will even be happy again."<br>"I don't want to recover. I want to cease to exist, now and forever. That's the only way to end my torment."<br>"We'll make the demons pay for what they did to you. Together. then we can talk about this again." And Zacharel would once again deny him.<br>"If you don't kill me, I'll kill myself. You know what will happen to me then."<br><br><b>My Reaction:</b><br>Oh Gena Showalter,<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/333415.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Page 166: -Anna's surprise-<br><br>To her utter shock, he smiled. Smiled! Lips curving up, straight white teeth revealed, dimples out in full glory. Yes, dimples. Awareness burned and blistered, a storm inside her. He was... He was... utterly magnificent.<br><br><b>My Reaction:</b><br><br><i>HE HAS DIMPLES</i>!!!! O.O<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368885ra/721453.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Page 240-254: -Zacharel's "Secret Friends"-<br><br>"Hey man, you got a light?" a male voice said.<br>Zacharel jolted to attention. the male stood in fron of him, a cigarette balanced between his lips.<br>He stood as tall as Zacharel, with hair so thick and luxurious any woman would covet it. The mass was a symphony of colors, shades of flax interspaced with caramel, chocolate and coffee. His eyes were a deep, fathomless blue, and his hauntingly lovely face something out of a catalog--or the heavens-- and completely at odds with his warrior's body.<br>Finally.<br>Annabelle gasped as if she had just spotted something precious, and Zacharel could only gnash his teeth in irritation.<br><br>"Pretty female. She yours?"<br>"Yes." Zacharel's tone shouted <i>so back off</i>.<br>Paris, keeper of the demon of Promiscuity, grinned slowly and with a satisfaction that only increased Zacharel's irritation. "She mute?"<br><br>*several pages later*<br><br>"I thought--" Her words were cut off as gunfire erupted. The horrible clang of metal against metal--then metal popping through flesh and into bone. Grunts and groans sounded. Shock and confusion blasted through her, holding her immobile. War had broken out, but all Annabelle could do was stand there, clutching the collar of Zacharel's robe. <br>"Friends of yours?" she asked.<br>"Yes. Their timing leaves something to be desired. They should have burst into the office much earlier," he added more loudly.<br>"Hey!" someone said. "We got up here as fast as we could."<br>"Then you need more training." Zacharel growled.<br><br>*one page later*<br><br>Annabelle spun. Smears of blood covered the walls and floor, though she could tell someone had tried to wipe them away. Other than that, there was no sign that a battle had taken place. Four bloodstained male warriors and the three females stood in the center of the room, each studying her with avid interest.<br>She would have studied them right back, but then she caught sight of Burden, still at his desk, his cheek pressed into the surface and a blade poised at the center of his neck, between two ridges of spine.<br>A horribly scarred man held that blade with a steady hand. "What do you want me to do with him, angel?"<br>"My men will come and collect him. We have questions, and he has answers."<br>"You said your men were not here," Burden gritted out.<br>Zacharel smiled the cruelest of his grins. "And they are not. Yet. I told you I brought no angels with me, and unlike you, I'm a man of my word. But I didn't make any promises about demons, did I? Allow me to introduce you to the Lords of the Underworld."<br><br><b>My Reaction:</b><br>Squeeeeeeeeee!!! The Lords!!! Oh Baby, it's the Lords!!!! &gt;.&lt;<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380780833ra/3122482.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368885ra/721454.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368885ra/721455.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And now that it's over....<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/670000.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380363289ra/714547.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368885ra/721456.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/333415.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368885ra/721457.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>*Composes self* Gena Showalter, you've outdone yourself once again, I really loved Wicked Nights, and I'm looking forward to <i>Beauty Awakened</i> :D<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380365801ra/717948.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>FANGIRLING? <i>MEEEE</i>?? Why, yes... Yes I am! <div id="review_383698650" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/383698650" />
    <a title="Kelly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8336973-kelly"><img alt="Kelly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1339138596p2/8336973.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/383698650?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly" href="/user/show/8336973-kelly">Kelly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/14731827-wicked-nights">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8336973-kelly?shelf=are-you-f-cking-kidding-me">are-you-f-cking-kidding-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8336973-kelly?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer383698650" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4571201647390043210">HOW has this book gotten so many 4 and 5 star reviews? The characters were flat and underdeveloped, the dialogue didn't flow, the sex scenes were lukewarm at best, the overuse of ellipses (...) throughout the book bugged the crap out of me, and the "and oh"s plaguing the book--all 16 of them--were highly annoying. <br/><br/>Like this: <br/>"A long, white robe draped him, somehow displaying his incredible strength, and oh, oh, oh, but he had brought the chill of the Arctic with him." <br/><br/>All those "oh"s are unneces</span>
  <span id="freeText4571201647390043210" style="display:none">HOW has this book gotten so many 4 and 5 star reviews? The characters were flat and underdeveloped, the dialogue didn't flow, the sex scenes were lukewarm at best, the overuse of ellipses (...) throughout the book bugged the crap out of me, and the "and oh"s plaguing the book--all 16 of them--were highly annoying. <br /><br />Like this: <br />"A long, white robe draped him, somehow displaying his incredible strength, and oh, oh, oh, but he had brought the chill of the Arctic with him." <br /><br />All those "oh"s are unnecessary and quite frankly, jarred me out the flow of reading. Now am I being a little nitpicky? Probably. But I can overlook stuff like this if the writing is solid, and unfortunately, Ms. Showalter's writing just isn't.<br /><br />All that stuff aside, the WORST part of this book was the purple prose, most of which didn't even make a damn lick of sense. <br /><br />An actual quote from the book:<br />"Her tongue rolled against his, bringing with it the tastes of summer: berries dipped in cream, newly blooming roses and sultry midnights."<br /><br />Seriously? Showalter's comparing the taste of Annabelle's tongue to "sultry midnights"? ...SERIOUSLY?? That's AWFUL writing right there, not to mention it doesn't make any freaking sense.<br /><br />How about this one:<br />"A decadent fire consumed her in seconds, burning her up."<br /><br />A fire cannot be decadent! This is absurd, and makes me wonder if Ms. Showalter even knows the meaning of the word.<br /><br />I was not impressed with the first book in the LOTU series, but I was willing to give the author another try. I should've stuck with my gut and avoided this one, like I will do from now on with ALL of Gena Showalter's books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4571201647390043210" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_303383571" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/303383571" />
    <a title="Exina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5309539-exina"><img alt="Exina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580809437p2/5309539.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/303383571?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Exina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Exina" href="/user/show/5309539-exina">Exina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=adventures">adventures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=something-is-missing">something-is-missing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=expected-more">expected-more</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=cliches">cliches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=gods-and-goddesses">gods-and-goddesses</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer303383571" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13768726170995847984"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>What we want is not always what we need.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><b>2.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Zacharel’s appearance in <i>The Darkest Seduction</i> really intrigued me to read his story. I pre-ordered his book in January, and after months of waiting, I was looking forward to knowing "ultracold" Zacharel's behaviour in romantic situations...<br/><i>Wicked Nights</i> is the first installment of the <i>Angels of the Dark</i> series, which is a <i>Lords of the Underworld</i> spin-off. <br/><br/><b>Zacharel</b> was always enigmatic, and although in his book I get to know a lot of t</span>
  <span id="freeText13768726170995847984" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>What we want is not always what we need.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><b>2.5 stars</b><br /><br />Zacharel’s appearance in <i>The Darkest Seduction</i> really intrigued me to read his story. I pre-ordered his book in January, and after months of waiting, I was looking forward to knowing "ultracold" Zacharel's behaviour in romantic situations...<br /><i>Wicked Nights</i> is the first installment of the <i>Angels of the Dark</i> series, which is a <i>Lords of the Underworld</i> spin-off. <br /><br /><b>Zacharel</b> was always enigmatic, and although in his book I get to know a lot of things about him, I still don’t feel him close to me. <br />It is absolutely Zacharel’s book. The story revolves around his life, his deeds, and his future. <br />Someone wants to take revenge on him, wants him to pay for a deed he was forced to do long time ago. Although Zacharel did his best, he unintentionally hurt this person. Since then, he suffers extremely because of it, and is sentenced to slow death himself.<br />Meanwhile, his Deity wants to teach him a lesson about the true essence of their mission, their true task. Zacharel hopes to be a member of the Elite Seven, but as yet he is not aware of the basic idea of being an angel. So the lesson is necessary. First it seems too cruel, but when the Deity explains it, it is so clear, so obvious. <br /><br />At the beginning of the story, I felt like <b>Annabelle</b> was a catalyst, a tool for starting and keeping the events in motion. She is not his equal as a main character. <br />She also suffers from this inequality in the story, from a different aspect, of course. Fortunately, she has the strength to become an equal partner of Zacharel. She is brave, smart, funny, and observant. <br />Annabelle has spirit; she is filled with hope, she never gives up. I loved her teasing, and nicknames for Zacharel.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Look, Winged Wonder. Get me out of here, then we’ll hammer out the details about where I’m staying, okay?”<br />“Winged Wonder,” he said, nodding. “I find that I do not mind that one. It fits.”<br />“Captain Modesty fits better,” she muttered.<br />“I disagree. Winged Wonder is clearly the better choice for a man such as me.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>Secondary characters</b><br />The warrior angels, Thane, Xerxes, Bjorn and Koldo in Zacharel’s army are very interesting characters.  I enjoyed their little insults toward Zacharel. As the story progresses, the insults disappear, and are replaced by respect for their leader.<br />The appearance of the Lords of the Underworld is spectacular! I love them so much!<br /><br /><b>Some problems</b><br />● The plot is well-built, but its fluidity and rhythm is broken by some elongated chapters and episodes, such as the chapter about Zacharel and Annabelle’s conversation about kisses, another chapter about their bargain of kisses, and a further chapter about their first kiss. <br /><br />● There is only one twist in the story, but that one is shocking. The awaited resolution-scene comes too late, only at the end. The fight with the antagonist is too short, too hasty.<br /><br />● I love the world Gena Showalter has created in the <i>Lords of the Underworld</i> series, because it is unique. Usually she doesn’t adopt clichés or popular images. But in here there some annoying things, such as the delineation of the Deity as an old man; the minion demons are sitting on humans’ shoulders and whispering incitements into their ears; ooh, and the demonic appearance of Annabelle disappears when she calms down, just like the Hulk...<br /><br />● The erotic scenes are kind of boring and faint. They are moderate and mannered: now you, then me, your turn, my turn, etc. Something is missing, maybe the heat. I didn’t feel the “thing” I should have felt as a reader.<br /><br />● The dialogues are witty, but I’m used to more humorous scenes in Gena Showalter’s books.<br />Romance, drama, and action are in appropriate amount in the novel, but their presentment is often superficial and depthless. <br /><br /><b>The cover</b><br />The cover is beautiful. The models are perfectly fit the main characters’ appearances. So far, for me it is the cover of the year.<br /><br /><a href="http://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/Wicked-Nights" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13768726170995847984" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_297616293" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/297616293" />
    <a title="Kate" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2786465-kate"><img alt="Kate" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350570834p2/2786465.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/297616293?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kate" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kate" href="/user/show/2786465-kate">Kate</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/14731827-wicked-nights">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2786465-kate?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer297616293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer698618697007938482">Maybe the worst book I have read this year. I'm no literary expert, I read fluff, smut, smuff, I read romance, scifi, fantasy, urban fantasy and I'll be the first to admit my tastes aren't very glamorous. I'm not that hard to please... So when I pick up a book like this and it is so resoundingly awful, I feel it is my duty to let everyone know. I wanted to put this book down when I was 70% of the way in, which is very very rare for me. I ended up finishing it just so I could write this scathing </span>
  <span id="freeText698618697007938482" style="display:none">Maybe the worst book I have read this year. I'm no literary expert, I read fluff, smut, smuff, I read romance, scifi, fantasy, urban fantasy and I'll be the first to admit my tastes aren't very glamorous. I'm not that hard to please... So when I pick up a book like this and it is so resoundingly awful, I feel it is my duty to let everyone know. I wanted to put this book down when I was 70% of the way in, which is very very rare for me. I ended up finishing it just so I could write this scathing review.<br /><br />In general, this author tries to be gritty, dirty and bad, she was trying to write this story about the ugly side of heaven... or soemthing in that vein. She's too cutesy, and fluffy, and it didn't work. It was like she was trying to be JR Ward or Ilona Andrews, but just paled in comparison.<br /><br />First, the circumstances that got Annabelle into that institute for the criminally insane were just dumb. On the day she turned 18, this girl supposedly killed her parents with a knife and chopped their bodies up (in daylight), then she called 911 and sat over her brother until they came. They got her because she had a knife in her hand that she had grabbed to protect herself, after her parents were murdered. First of all, the knife would have had no blood on the blade, and even if it were cleaned, a forensics lab would have been able to tell you that. Even though she had just turned 18, any good lawyer would have had her tried as a minor. Also, when you're in "jail" or in Annabell's case, an institute for the criminally insane, you do not have your hands cuffed behind your back on a regular basis, unless you're being transported somewhere. That sort of treatment is considered abusive because it can do permanent damage to your ligaments. In a criminally insane institution, you would have been cuffed in front with leather straps, and your hands would have been linked by a chain to your cuffed ankles. They also tend to have cameras everywhere, and I doubt that there would be so much abuse going on between the administrators and the patients.<br /><br />Also, if you were randomly attached by demons no one else could see, don't you think people would wonder about the random cuts and scrapes you got, seemingly out of mid-air?<br /><br />Economics and punishment in the Angel world also made no sense. Why the hell would an angel have to pay to live in a "cloud" or to live anywhere? And seriously, the author could not have come up with something less simple for them to live inside of, instead of a cloud? Why are bad angels punished with violence? That also made no sense. I think we all learned over the past few thousand years that flogging doesn't really solve anything... especially for fast-healing angels that have a very high pain tolerance.<br /><br />I also don't believe for a second that if an angel is anything like a human, how one like Zacherel could have gone through thousands of years of his life without once having had sex (or at least a friggin' hard on). He was an adolescent once, one with mary-sue like abilities and he had a writhing mass of humans and otherworldly beings at his beck and call... Yeah, no.<br /><br />Also, I did not once understand how he could have been attracted to Annabelle. Annabelle was a bitchy, angsty, whiny, adolescent child who was supposedly 22 years old. Apparently Zach's essentia latched onto her, and he didn't have a choice. Annabelle was such an awful person with no attractive or redeemable qualities. She was also incredibly dumb, anytime Zach told her he was leaving a room, she would get all angsty and wonder if that was him dumping her. Ahhh my goodness, I wanted to grab some bouncy balls and tape them to her anatomy, because I knew she didn't have the ability to grow a pair.<br /><br />She would have been the most angsty and emo person to have ever lived, if it was not for Zacharel and his QQing over his dead brother. Did it annoy anyone else that he had this black spot growing on his chest, but didn't really care? At least he stood up for himself at times and sort of tried to shake the dumb out of Annabelle.<br /><br />I also know I don't need to read any of the other books by this author because she introduced her other characters to the reader, and I hated them all. So that's a relief!<br /><br />Okay, there were other things about this book that I didn't like, but I think I am done with this review. I am going to go read some paranormal romance that is actually good now, bye!</span>
  <a data-text-id="698618697007938482" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/239709794?book_show_action=true">Nov 25, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=booty-snatching">booty-snatching</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer239709794" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18365035604306987335"><b>Posted on<a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.ca/2012/06/review-wicked-nights-by-gena-showalter.html' rel='nofollow noopener'> Under the Covers</a></b><br/><br/>From the amazing author who brought you the Lords of the Underworld comes a new world were angels toe the line between darkness and light. In WICKED NIGHTS, the first book of the ANGELS OF THE DARK series, Gena Showalter introduces a virgin angel named Zacharel. Burdened by the Deity to be the leader of a group of badass angels, Zacharel is forced to lead and receive punishment for any misdeeds they commit. In this group there is Thane, Bjorn, Xerxes and Koldo. All of w</span>
  <span id="freeText18365035604306987335" style="display:none"><b>Posted on<a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.ca/2012/06/review-wicked-nights-by-gena-showalter.html" rel="nofollow noopener"> Under the Covers</a></b><br /><br />From the amazing author who brought you the Lords of the Underworld comes a new world were angels toe the line between darkness and light. In WICKED NIGHTS, the first book of the ANGELS OF THE DARK series, Gena Showalter introduces a virgin angel named Zacharel. Burdened by the Deity to be the leader of a group of badass angels, Zacharel is forced to lead and receive punishment for any misdeeds they commit. In this group there is Thane, Bjorn, Xerxes and Koldo. All of which are tortured souls waiting to exact revenge on someone or something.<br /><br /> I thoroughly enjoyed this book! I have been a fan of Showalter for some time now and firmly believe that her writing has improved with each book. I noticed this in her last release, THE DARKEST SEDUCTION, but in WICKED NIGHTS, Showalter really shows her strength and growth as a writer. Her writing has become more descriptive, more tighter and the proof is in the pages. Gena has been working her butt off and you can totally see the improvements in each subsequent book.<br /><br />Probably the biggest reason I loved this book is because I adored the hero and heroine. Zacharel is a virgin – need I say more? And Annabelle is a woman who has faced a tough life, but doesn’t allow her past hurts to haunt her. I adored her spunk and fiery spirit and added to Zacharel’s more serious side results in some hilarious dialogue. Here, case in point:<br /><br />Annabelle alternately marveled at the change in him and at the luminosity of the full moon. Other humans gave him a wide berth, nearly flattening themselves against the building walls to widen the distance between them. Annabelle danced around him, grinning. “Can I just say what a bad boy you are right now?”<br /> “Of course you can. You just did.”<br />“No, I mean – Oh, never mind, you spoiled it. “ Her lips dipped into a pout. <br /><br /> Zacharel is adorable!<br /><br />While I thought the book lacked the thread that should have pulled the plot forward, I found that I really enjoyed the ending. Showalter pulls a little twist at the ending that I really enjoyed and it really stirred the pot up! For fans of the LOTU, there are a lot of cameos in this book. You’ll be happy to note that Paris and Lucien and some of the women and more make regular appearances. It was hilarious to read Annabelle’s reaction to Paris’ hotness.<br /><br /> Now I am jonesing for a taste of Koldo and Xerxes. Out of all the other angels, they stood out to me the most. If Showalter continues to write like this for her next books, there is no doubt that the Angels of the Dark series will be just as successful as the Lords of the Underworld. Watch out now, Lords ‘cause the Angels have arrived!<br /><br />*Early Review Copy provided by author </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3324771992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7129969069443071999">"Wicked Nights" is the first book in the "Angels of the Dark"-series and are also related to "Lords of the Underworld"-series.Gena Showalter presents another bunch of sexy tortured warrior Angels,irresistible romance and hard-core action and magic and a wonderful twist that i actually predicted!Annabelle Miller was a normal girl until a demon from hell killed her parents and then marked her as his own.Being a suspect of her parents murder she gets locked up in a mental institution.The ice-cold A</span>
  <span id="freeText7129969069443071999" style="display:none">"Wicked Nights" is the first book in the "Angels of the Dark"-series and are also related to "Lords of the Underworld"-series.Gena Showalter presents another bunch of sexy tortured warrior Angels,irresistible romance and hard-core action and magic and a wonderful twist that i actually predicted!Annabelle Miller was a normal girl until a demon from hell killed her parents and then marked her as his own.Being a suspect of her parents murder she gets locked up in a mental institution.The ice-cold Angel warrior Zachariel kills the demons located there and decides to save Annabelle after feeling a undeniable pull towards her.Together they have to slay the demon of Unforgiveness to finally free her from his poison.<br /><br />Annabelle Miller is half-japanese and very strong and brave when it came to her circumstances.I mean fate had been everything but good towards her,and she refused to dwell on the past.If it were me i would be ballshit crazy if all that shit happened to me!I love how she opens up to Zachariel`s world,and how she falls for the golden hearted man he is.She comes to love him irrevocably and i love it that she knew that he also felt the same before he even knew it.<br />Zachariel is a Deity warrior and a very beautiful Angel who haven`t felt any emotion at all for centuries ever since he had to kill his twin-brother Hadraniel.He is also a virgin,which i found so romantic!It was fun watching in the past books how he was so confused about the love the Lords felt for their women and i so longed for him to get a woman of his own and fall head over heels!Annabelle quickly becomes his whole world,she teaches him to love and sacrifice and the goodness of humanity.I cried at the scene where he humbled himself in front of her down his knees,crying to her stomach and begging for forgiveness!Ahh how i wanted to hug him to pieces!<br /><br />I am so intrigued by Koldo,Thane,Xerxes and Bjorn-i mean all these warriors are sexy as hell and their dark attitudes only makes them more irresistible!Paris,Strider,Kaia,Amun,Haidee,Lucien and Anya from the LOTU series also appeared which made me giddy as hell,just jumped up and down in my room!Paris makes my heart sing everytime he appears!Oh,and one thing i realized about this book was that the sex-scenes aren`t as detailed as in the authors other books,why is that?I loved this book either way,it was all i could expect from the Queen of paranormal romance genre Gena Showalter.</span>

<div id="review_228467743" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/228467743" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5176570-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1337864692p2/5176570.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/228467743?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/5176570-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=aint-he-sweet">aint-he-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=badass-hero">badass-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=angelic-delights">angelic-delights</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=cocky-hero">cocky-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=gena-showalter">gena-showalter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=demons-do-it-for-me">demons-do-it-for-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=frau-badass">frau-badass</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=fated-to-be-mated">fated-to-be-mated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5176570-melanie?shelf=hey-look-what-i-can-do">hey-look-what-i-can-do</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer228467743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16267380023500483580"><b>5+ stars</b>!!! Zacharel = HOT HOT HOT (even when he's oh so cold...)<br/><br/>'Wicked Nights' heralds the first in Gena Showalter's new series 'Angels of the Dark', a spin-off of her wildly popular 'Lords of the Underworld' books, and (IMHO) she has definitely hit it out of the park with this one. I absolutely <i>loved</i> it!<br/><br/>Paranormal romance used to be my all-time favorite, numero uno, top choice when it came to reading... and it still is to some extent. However, it seems like the genre is just so overloaded wit</span>
  <span id="freeText16267380023500483580" style="display:none"><b>5+ stars</b>!!! Zacharel = HOT HOT HOT (even when he's oh so cold...)<br /><br />'Wicked Nights' heralds the first in Gena Showalter's new series 'Angels of the Dark', a spin-off of her wildly popular 'Lords of the Underworld' books, and (IMHO) she has definitely hit it out of the park with this one. I absolutely <i>loved</i> it!<br /><br />Paranormal romance used to be my all-time favorite, numero uno, top choice when it came to reading... and it still is to some extent. However, it seems like the genre is just so overloaded with mediocre and crap books these days, it's hard to find and latch onto something exciting and <i>new</i>. That's why I've been branching out of my comfort zone and have thankfully discovered some <u>ah-may-zing</u> reads in other romance sub-genres (*cough Kristen Ashley cough*). Oh, I've still got my favorite go-to, auto-buy paranormal romance authors and Gena Showalter is among them, but sometimes their books even fall a bit short off the mark (*ahem* 'The Darkest Seduction'). So when I found out GS was coming out with a LOTU spin-off I was both super excited and a tad wary. Turns out, there was no need to be wary. 'Wicked Nights' was fresh, exciting, sexy, action-packed and one of the <u>best</u> books Gena Showalter has written to date. <br /><br />We first met aloof, sexy badass Angel Zacharel in 'The Darkest Secret' and it was a panty-melting experience. His arrogance and continued cold-indifference have landed him in trouble with the Deity and he now finds himself leading an army of badass Angel misfits. (ROWR! - There are a LOT of tortured bad-boys to love here!!) These guys have been f*ck-ups for a while and this is their last chance - if Zacharel and his demon-fighting crew of Angelic warriors don't manage to redeem themselves within a year then they are Fallen. Trouble is, there is little to no respect between Zacharel and his new army, and they are struggling (and pretty much failing) to work together. When they are called in to defeat a horde of demons attacking an institution for the criminally insane, Zacharel meets a beautiful inmate, Annabelle, who manages to crack his ice-cold facade. <i>She</i> is the intended target of the demons and while he can't understand <i>why</i> he's drawn to her, he decides to free her anyway... And when Zacharel begins to feel for the first time in eons, trust and respect begins to grow between him and his warriors.<br /><br />There were a lot of twists and turns in 'Wicked Nights', and the last 100 pages were especially gripping. I'll admit that I believed I knew where the book was heading fairly early on - and it <i>does</i> indeed turn out somewhat like I expected... but it also doesn't. Showalter manages to pack in a few unexpected surprises and follows through with a thrilling climax. When all was said and done, I was left completely satisfied and antsy for more! I can't wait for Koldo's story - bring on <u>more</u> 'Angels of the Dark'!<br /><br /><br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="16267380023500483580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=angels-and-demons">angels-and-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=heart-warming-stories">heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=pure-addiction">pure-addiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=slow-burn">slow-burn</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1890340864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10512359424345409948"><b>4.25/5 stars</b> <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“You are mine,” he rasped. “Only ever mine. I accept all that you are, and we can be together.” </b>
</blockquote> <br/> <br/>I cant believe that this is my first Gena Showalter book! Everyone takes about her <i>Lords of the Underworld</i> series and here I am only just starting her spin-off series. I totally understand why everyone is addicted to these books, <i>Wicked Nights</i> was amazing! It was sweet, funny and had angels in it!! Angels are by far my favourite paranormal being to read about, but I just haven't fou</span>
  <span id="freeText10512359424345409948" style="display:none"><b>4.25/5 stars</b> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“You are mine,” he rasped. “Only ever mine. I accept all that you are, and we can be together.” </b>
</blockquote> <br> <br>I cant believe that this is my first Gena Showalter book! Everyone takes about her <i>Lords of the Underworld</i> series and here I am only just starting her spin-off series. I totally understand why everyone is addicted to these books, <i>Wicked Nights</i> was amazing! It was sweet, funny and had angels in it!! Angels are by far my favourite paranormal being to read about, but I just haven't found many angel books that Ive really connected to. The angels in this book are sexy, edgy and super cute (although they'd probably kill me for saying so)!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452810465ra/17746972.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Zacharel is the commander of a brutal angel army who all seem to be on the brink of falling. They're all a force to be reckoned with but Zacharel is by far the most likely to lose his wings as he is seen as too cold hearted, dangerous and too ruthless of heaven. He has never cared about collateral damage or taking human lives whilst destroying demons...until one vulnerable human unleashes desire from deep within him. Zacharel experiences desire like he never has before and will try everything to claim the human for as his own.<br><br>Annabelle Miller has spent the last four years locked away in a mental institute for the criminally insane accused of killing her parents. Nobody believes her when she talks about the demon who killed her parents or the other demons that seem to follow her everywhere. Zacharel might be her only salvation, but their relationship grows to become much more than just Zacharel protecting Annabelle. Their desire for each other grows, but how can an angel love someone who has been claimed by a demon.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Look, Winged Wonder. Get me out of here, then we'll hammer out the details about where I'm staying. Okay?"<br>"Winged Wonder," he said, nodding. "I find that I do not mind that one. It fits."<br>"Captain Modesty fits better," she muttered.<br>"I disagree. Winged Wonder is clearly the better choice for a man such as me."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>This was just such a charming book! It was addictive, funny and constantly entertaining. </b>The world that Gena Showalter created is so rich and phenomenally detailed, I was thinking about it long after it was finished. The angels were so uniquely created and described. There were unique aspects about them that I've never read before and I absolutely loved diving into the world and getting to know all about the paranormal beings and magic system. Usually I get bored about history, politics and backstories but I was drawn into every word about these angels. <b>I am well and truly hooked! </b><br><br>I have no specific negative comments about this book, however, it did take me a while to get connected to the story. I think this was may be to do with me being extremely busy whilst I was reading the book so I never had time to just sit down and get fully immersed in the story. There was also a lot of history and hierarchy explanations at the start which took a while for me to fully get my head around. But this really wasn't a big issue for me and overall, I really enjoyed the book! I just wish I could have sat down and binge read it instead of being constantly interrupted (how rude of life to interrupt my reading time)!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“You know, you’re pretty when you smile,” she said, patting the side of his cheek. <br>“Fierce, woman. I am fierce.” <br>“If you say so.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The romance in this book was definitely a slow burn, but the angst and tension was there from the start. They had an enormous amount of chemistry as well as great banter, some super sweet moments and an overwhelming desire to protect each other. <br><br>At the start of the book, Zacharel is basically emotionless and has a very hard time understanding human fancies, emotions and vulnerabilities. It was actually hilarious to read about him stumbling over these newfound emotions and desires after meeting Annabelle. He developed so much over the book and by the end he was sweet, protective but still hot as hell! I thought he was such an adorable character and I loved him to pieces! His character also meshed so well with Annabelle (who I also love) because she was a strong, stubborn and feisty women with a heart of gold. Together they made such a perfect character and I revelled in every moment they spent together and how much they developed throughout the book.<br><br>Even though I haven't read the <i>Lords of the Underworld series</i>, I found it super easy to get to know the characters and understand where they fit in the story. The minor characters were such a grea influence on the book and brought so much more fun and entertainment. Whilst I was reading and loving Annabelle and Zacharel's story, at the same time I was excited to read about these other characters. Without a doubt I'm continuing this series as well as the author's other series.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“It shall be my pleasure to remedy it. First, it is not your strength or your speed that draws me. It's your...everything. Your laugh, your wit, your emotions and the way they change. Your courage, your sweetness, your near obsessive delight in cookies. Second, you are indeed a prize. You've made me want what no one else ever had. A communion of bodies."</b>
</blockquote></span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText11022399376098895108" style="display:none"><br />Spoiler Free Review<br />4 STARS out of 5<br />Genre: Adult Paranormal Romance/Urban Fantasy<br />Series: Book #1 in Angels of the Dark series<br /><br /><i> Zacharel is cold blooded, he feels no emotion. <b>HOWEVER</b> one human girl will warm his blood and bring a passion that will burn him to his soul.</i> In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12900491.Wicked_Nights__Angels_of_the_Dark___1_" title="Wicked Nights (Angels of the Dark, #1) by Gena Showalter" rel="nofollow noopener">Wicked Nights</a><br /><br />The Deity has claimed Zacharel too dangerous. His cold hearted mentality will leave him wingless if he does not change his ways. Now with a gang of angel misfits Zacharel must learn to melt the ice in his chest while teaching his misfit army of Angels to do the same by showing compassion and respect for human life. <br /><br />Annabelle Miller has spent the last four years of her life in a hospital for the criminally insane for the murder of her parents. Problem is Annabelle did not commit the crime. A demon did, of course when she tells the police " A monster did it" that does not help her case. A Demon king wants Annabelle and he sends out demons to track her on a regular basis. Fighting has become her lifestyle and she refuses to let the demons win. So when an Angel appears she holds out a little hope that he will save her.<br /><b>How can Zacharel save Anna when he has not felt emotions such as sympathy for over a millennium?<br />And how long will it take for him to realize that they share a common enemy?<br /><i><br />Soon the ice cold Angel with the piercing green eyes will learn that love is more powerful than anything he has EVER experienced.</i></b><br /><br /><u>Thoughts</u><br />The book started pretty slow for me but when it picked up it really got my attention. The twist was good though i saw it coming about 2 seconds before it happened.<br /><b>Annabelle-</b> Anna has become one of my fave PNR heroines. She was fun fierce and female just the way I like them! She kicked all ass and was willing to make the ultimate sacrifice if need be.<br /><b>Zacharel-</b> Started off very cold and at times ignorant. And i guess with some things he really was ignorant to his credit he is considered to be like most Angels innocent and nonchalant. However Anna heated his cold blood quickly making him crave things he never knew he wanted. Like Love, Sex and Cookies.<br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Likeable<br />Writing Style- Good<br />Plot/Storyline- Good<br />Steam Factor- Low to Slow Simmer/Moderately Steamy<br />Overall- I liked it! <br /><b><br />Now go forth and read.
